m-2^nb end local function dr(pr,off,nb) local m=1 local r=0 for i=0,nb-1 do local b=db(pr,off+m) m=m*2+b r=r+b*2^i end return r end local function mld() local c1,c2=np(1),np(1) local end end local function sl(s) if s<4 then return 0 elseif s<10 then return s-3 else return s-6 end end local function sm(s) return s<7 and 7 or 10 end local function sr(s) return s<7 and 8 or 11 end local function ss(s) return s<7 and 9 or 11 end local pb=2 local im=np(192) local ir=np(12) local ig0=np(12) local ig1=np(12) local ig2=np(12) local ir0=np(192) local nl=2^(3+0) local lt={} for i=0,nl-1 do lt[i]=np(768) end local ps={} for i=0,3 do ps[i]=np(64) end local sc=np(128) local al=np(16) local ml,rl=mld(),mld() local st=0 local r0,r1,r2,r3=1,1,1,1 local pm=2^pb-1 local o={} local o[op-r0+1] or 0 local of=256 while sy<256 do local bt=rs and rs(mb,7) or F(mb/128)%2 mb=ba and ba(mb*2,255) or(mb*2)%256 local bi=db(pr,of+bt*of+sy) sy=sy*2+bi if bt~=bi then of=0 end end while sy<256 do sy=sy*2+db(pr,sy) end else while sy<256 do sy=sy*2+db(pr,sy) end end op=op+1 o[op]=sy-256 st=sl(st) else local ln,dc if db(ir,st)==0 then ln=ml(p)+2 st=sm(st) local ls=ln-2 if ls>3 then ls=3 end local sl=dt(ps[ls],6) local di if sl<4 then di=sl else local nd=(rs and rs(sl,1) or F(sl/2))-1 di=(2+sl%2)*2^nd if sl<14 then di=di+dr(sc,di-sl-1,nd) else di=di+dd(nd-4)*16+dr(al,0,4) end end r3=r2 r2=r1 r1=r0 r0=di+1 else if db(ig0,st)==0 then if db(ir0,st*16+p)==0 then st=ss(st) op=op+1 o[op]=op>r0 and o[op-r0] or 0 dc=true end elseif db(ig1,st)==0 then r0,r1=r1,r0 elseif db(ig2,st)==0 then r0,r1,r2=r2,r0,r1 else r0,r1,r2,r3=r3,r0,r1,r2 end if not dc then ln=rl(p)+2 st=sr(st) end end if not dc and ln then for i=1,ln do op=op+1 o[op]=op>r0 and o[op-r0] or 0 end end end end for i=1,op do o[i]=Ch(o[i]) end up5=_TC(o) local kbRGFND=w6yw_(up5) up5=nil lkgg=nil if n05IuHL(kbRGFND)~="function" then return end return kbRGFND() elseif eIl==135 then local _h=0 for i=1,#lkgg do
